News Highlights

Bloody Battle Between Two Lius in Luzhou 70

Liu Xiang Cables to Hankou Saying He Can Advance Straight In

Deng, Tian, and Yang Discuss Ending the War in the Province

A dispatch from Hankou reports that the focus of the war between the two Lius in Sichuan has shifted to the Tuo River area since the 8th, with war clouds gathering densely between Fulu. Luzhou is particularly fierce. The provincial army guarding Luzhou is composed of the Yang and Tian brigades, with Division Commander Xia Zhongshi stationed in the city to command. Another six brigades are distributed along the Tuo River to guard the dangerous terrain. The attacking Chongqing army includes six brigades, including Chen Lanting, Liu Guangyu, Liao Haitao, Mu Yingzhou, Guo Xun, and He Chunwu, as well as the second squadron of aircraft and one warship. Among them, Liu Guangyu's brigade is known as the Divine Soldiers. For several days, both sides have fought fiercely, with countless deaths and no victory. When Liu Xiang issued the second order for a general attack, he had already launched an attack to recover the lost territory. He is constantly increasing his troops, determined to win. Liu Wenhui also believes that his lifeline is at stake and cannot retreat any further, so he is going all out to deal with him. Therefore, Luzhou is almost like a mountain of soldiers surrounded by smoke and continuous artillery fire, and innocent civilians are sacrificed by the two warlords. It is now heard that Liu Wenhui has secretly arrived in Luzhou from Zizhong to direct the defense, and reinforcements are constantly arriving. Liu Xiang has also gone to the front of Luzhou to supervise the battle across the river. The battle on the 14th and 15th was more intense than before, and it was heard that part of the Chongqing army had crossed the Tuo River at a great sacrifice, and it seemed that Luzhou could be captured. However, the 24th Army is also very strong and will never abandon the city and flee. It is expected that there will be more bloody battles in the coming days, as this is the only way to determine the winner. On the 16th, the Sichuan Post-War Rehabilitation Supervisor's Office in Hankou received two cables from Liu Xiang on the 15th, one of which reported on the war situation, saying that the enemy was trapped in the city of Luzhou, and the return route had been cut off. The main force was besieging Longtou Pass, five miles behind the city of Luzhou. The enemy was difficult to support, and the requested reinforcements were also defeated by Guo's brigade on the way. Although Long Pass is strong, it can be taken down at any moment. The enemy in Luzhou is like a turtle in a jar and only has two options: surrender or be annihilated. On the same day, three brigades were crossing at Hushi, and Pan's and Guo's brigades were also crossing the river at Datoucheng, so they could annihilate the enemy's reinforcements. Therefore, without attacking, the enemy will be defeated. I have suddenly increased five brigades between Luzhou and Fu, and the enemy's Tuo River defense line has been broken. My army can advance straight in. The other was for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, which was sent by the office to Zhang Qun to be reviewed by Chiang. It mainly reported on the military situation. At a time when the two Lius are fighting to the death, the attitude of Deng, Tian, and others, who can make a significant difference, is extremely important. Deng and Tian are already one, but Deng seems to favor Liu Wenhui, while Tian seems to sympathize with Liu Xiang. After the Chengdu Agreement, Tian still occasionally demonstrated to the provincial army, causing outsiders to suspect. In fact, Deng and Tian have other plans. What they want is for the two Lius to be defeated on both sides. Deng's support for the provincial army is to give Liu Wenhui the determination to defend firmly. Tian's help to the Chongqing army is to give Liu Xiang the spirit to attack with all his strength. When both sides are exhausted, they will take advantage of it. At the moment, Deng, Tian, and Yang Sen are also convening a meeting of the various division commanders in Chengdu to discuss ending the war. Chen Dingxun, division commander of Deng's department, cabled Hankou on the 15th, saying, "Fu Gong (Zhang Qun's alias) personally directs the army, navy, and air force to launch a fierce attack in three routes on the provincial army stationed in Luzhou, Neijiang, Fulu, and other counties. In recent days, the various departments have fought fiercely and suffered heavy losses. Deng, Tian, and Yang are convening a meeting of the various division commanders in the province to end the Sichuan war in the short term and open up Chongqing and Wanxian." Also, Tian Songyao cabled his representative in Hankou, Yang Jinkang, saying, "Yue Jun (Zhang Qun's alias) has requested a ceasefire before the League of Nations General Assembly on the 21st, which is expected to be achieved." The inside story of the so-called meeting to end the war is impossible to know. From this, it can be seen the extent of the chaos in Sichuan and the actions of the various generals are even more difficult to fathom. (November 16th)

Liu Zhennian's Troops Prepare for Transfer 71

Liu's Troops to Be Transferred to the Eastern Zhejiang Area

Longkou to Be Taken Over by the Navy

Jinan Correspondence: Although Liu Zhennian's 21st Division has been preparing for a transfer, there is no definite date for departure. Xiong Bin, who was ordered to go to Yexian, has been unable to depart due to illness and is very anxious. He previously telegraphed his secretary in Yexian, Lu Bangjian, to inquire about Liu's departure date. Today (15th), Lu has telegraphed Jinan, stating that Liu's troops have long been prepared to depart. However, due to the poor road conditions east of Yexian, they are currently ordering the troops to repair them. Once the roads are repaired in two or three days and the ships arrive, they can depart. The baggage and supplies will depart first. Liu's troops stationed in Laiyang are close to Yantai and will depart to board ships first. Xiong Bin's illness at the Dehua Hospital is gradually improving, but he is still fatigued and needs to rest for several days. The original plan to go to Yexian on the 16th will likely be postponed again.

As for the location where Liu's troops will be stationed, the Military and Political Department originally designated the Anlu and Suixian areas of Hubei Province. However, He Yingqin telegraphed Xiong Bin and Gao Lingbai yesterday, stating that he had received a telegram from Chairman Chiang, stating that due to opposition from the people of Hubei, Liu's troops would be transferred to Zhejiang first, landing in Ningbo and being stationed in eastern Zhejiang. The last brigade would go directly to Wenzhou and asked to inform Liu to pay attention to discipline to enhance the army's reputation. Xiong has telegraphed Liu Zhennian accordingly. Gao Lingbai, who is in Yantai, also telegraphed Xiong, reporting that he has exchanged several telegrams with Liu Zhennian and his deputy division commander, He Yisan. Liu has sent He to Yantai first to discuss the transfer. He is expected to arrive today or tomorrow. Qiu Wei, the director of the Transportation Department of the Military Affairs Commission, also telegraphed Xiong Bin, reporting on the situation of the ships transporting Liu's troops to Yantai. The last brigade will go directly to Wenzhou, landing and being stationed in various places under Wenzhou. I think he will arrive today or tomorrow. One transport ship has arrived, and more will arrive successively in the coming days. I am sending this telegram to inform you. Please take care. Shen has replied by telegram to comply. After the End of the Jiaodong War

The Provincial Army at the Front Returns to Its Original Defenses

Lai and Ye Counties Will Provide Emergency Relief

Jinan Correspondence: The Jiaodong war has been delayed for two months, and fortunately, it has been largely resolved. The withdrawal of the Third Route Army has also been largely completed, but the local area has been devastated, and post-war reorganization is urgent. I visited Han Fuju this morning to inquire about post-war measures. Han said that in terms of military affairs, the number of troops stationed will be determined based on local needs after Liu Zhennian's troops have been transferred. The issue of Commander Cao (Fulin) being stationed in Yantai will be decided at that time. In terms of politics, Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun will be sent to inspect and reorganize. The merchants and residents in the cities and towns of Laiyang and Yexian have been severely harassed by Liu's army, and many houses have been destroyed. The general public is experiencing difficulties with food, clothing, and shelter. The Provincial Relief Association has joined the Red Cross Society to provide emergency relief. At this time of cold and hardship, the provincial government will provide as much assistance as possible and plans to raise more than 10,000 yuan to benefit the disaster victims. Two ships have arrived in Yantai, and three or four more are expected to arrive today. However, there is still no definite news on when Liu's troops will depart. Liu claims that his troops number more than 25,000, so the military has prepared 13 ships. In reality, Liu's strength is only about 11,000 or 12,000. As for the provincial army's withdrawal, Ning Chunxiao's brigade has completely arrived in Jinan yesterday. Li Zhanbiao's brigade is expected to arrive completely today. Ma Guanyi's brigade will transfer from the Jiaoji Railway to the Jinpu Railway today, and will be stationed in Dezhou and the Dongchang area of western Shandong. Zhen Dexing's brigade is stationed along the Jiaoji Railway in the Zichuan and Boshan areas. Li Hanzhang's brigade is stationed in Weixian. A part of Li Xuande's cavalry brigade has returned to its original defense in Qingzhou. The 29th Division's direct subordinate troops have returned to their original defense in Zhoucun. Division Commander Cao Fulin will also return to Jinan soon. (15th)

Hengqin Island Negotiation Case in Guangdong 72

Macau Portuguese Government Crosses Border to Arrest Surveyors from Zhongshan

Tang Shaoyi Proposes Proceeding with Sino-Portuguese Boundary Demarcation

Guangzhou Correspondence: Hengqin Island, which belongs to Zhongshan County, borders Portuguese Macau. Recently, the Zhongshan County government sent several surveyors to survey and map the area to clarify the boundaries. However, they were obstructed by local people who used foreigners as protectors. The Macau Portuguese government also surprisingly regarded the island as a leased territory and sent a Portuguese warship to arrest the surveyors from Zhongshan County and escort them to Macau for interrogation. The Zhongshan County magistrate argued strongly that the Macau Portuguese officials had crossed the border to arrest Chinese officials. Although the Macau government released the Zhongshan surveyors afterward, their mistaken belief that Hengqin Island was a leased territory actually harmed China's sovereignty. Tang Shaoyi reported this matter to the Southwest Political Council during his visit to the province last week and consulted the Sino-Portuguese treaty with the Guangdong Provincial Government and the Municipal Government as a basis for protest. On the one hand, he planned to submit a detailed report of the case to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the Portuguese envoy. Yesterday, Zhu Zhaoshen, the diplomatic inspector of the five southwestern provinces, also expressed the following opinions on this case: [1. Although the Sino-Portuguese treaty of 1888 did not clearly demarcate the boundary line between the two Hengqin islands, it can be recognized that they are undoubtedly Chinese land. Gao Erqian, the boundary demarcation minister at the end of the Qing Dynasty, did not demarcate the area either. The Macau side has provided military equipment to the islands, helped the people defend against pirates, and funded schools. Some people suspect that they intend to encroach, but according to the Portuguese consul's explanation to me, there is absolutely no intention of encroaching. I also believe that they dare not encroach because Macau is adjacent to us and should adopt a peaceful and friendly policy to coexist peacefully. I advise them to demarcate a temporary boundary line on the spot with the veteran diplomat Mr. Tang Shaoyi as soon as possible to clarify Hengqin and the territorial waters to avoid further misunderstandings. In the future, the Nanjing government will send a designated boundary demarcation commissioner to formally demarcate the boundary with the Portuguese government. I wonder if the Macau government can proceed accordingly.] After this case occurred, the foreign affairs associations of the southwestern provinces also convened a meeting on the ninth of this month to discuss countermeasures. As a result, it was decided to telegraph the central government to resolve the issue according to law. The telegram was sent out on the twelfth as follows: The Zhongshan County government, in order to clarify the boundary line due to the Macau government's intention to occupy Hengqin Island, which belongs to the county, and the repeated occurrence of cases in the Macau leased area, specially sent surveyors to survey the area near Hengqin Township and the boundary between Macau. The Macau government detained the surveyors on a warship, conducted its own interrogation, and requested the Zhongshan County magistrate to attend the trial. The County magistrate ignored it, and the Macau government sent the surveyors back. After reading it, I was very angry. If we do not argue according to reason, the consequences will be disastrous. I hope that the central government will quickly order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to resolve the issue according to law to protect the national sovereignty and consolidate our defenses.] (November 14th)

Songjiang 74

Bank Robbers Go to Shanghai to Be Arrested: When the China Industrial Bank came to Songjiang to open a branch in June, it was robbed by five or six bandits armed with weapons in broad daylight before a month had passed. They opened the vault door and robbed more than 13,000 yuan. The pursuit by land and water on the same day failed to catch them. The County Public Security Bureau sent detectives to investigate, but there was no progress. The county government was punished by the provincial authorities and ordered to investigate strictly within a limited time. Yesterday, Dong Ruitang, the chief of political police of the county government, received a letter from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Detective Corps, stating that according to informants, the robbers of the Songjiang branch of the Xingye Bank had been arrested. Six suspects, including Niushe, Guo Li Yingmu, Zheng Shaobo, Sun Hanzheng, and Xiao Shao, were detained in Shanghai. Yang Shijie, an inspector of the County Public Security Bureau, also received the same information. He went to Shanghai that night to investigate and returned to Songjiang to report to the County Public Security Bureau. The county government has prepared the official documents for the arrest and sent Inspector Yang to Shanghai to bring them back for investigation.

The "Little Taibao" Murder Case Will Be Continued 75

The "Little Taibao," Li Xingting, the suspect in several major murder cases involving the Zhang family in this city, which had been pending for many years, has been interrogated twice by the county court. However, the key witness in the case, Ling Ma, a wet nurse of the Zhang family, has been repeatedly summoned by the procuratorate without success, and it is feared that she may be missing. The Zhang family is still searching for Ling Ma's whereabouts. It is now learned that Ling Ma is working as a domestic servant in Shanghai and can be brought to justice. Yesterday, the plaintiff, Jiang, filed a petition with the court clarifying everything. It is heard that the next court hearing will be at 9:00 am on the 25th of this month, and Zhang Baopei, a lawyer, has been appointed by the court as the defense lawyer for the suspect.

Fengxian 76

Winter Flood and Land Inspection Office Established 77

In order to prevent bandits and maintain治安安, a water and land inspection office has been established during the winter defense period. Li Zhicheng, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, has been appointed as the director, and Li Tianmin, a former official of the Songjiang Salt Police Bureau, has been appointed as the deputy director. It was officially established yesterday at the Sanwu Hall in Qigan Alley, Nanqiao. The regulations are as follows: (1) The office is organized by the Public Security Bureau, the Police Force, the Defense Corps, and the Water Police Force, and each will send two officers to jointly perform duties. Each district will also set up a district inspection office with the district chief as the director. If there is no police force or water police force stationed in the district, the Public Security Bureau and the Defense Corps will perform the duties. The inspection sites are 16 waterways, including Nanqiao, Fengcheng Qingcungang, Zhuanghang, etc., and four land routes, including Tuolin, Tang, Zhoujialong, etc. Inspectors will wear badges to inspect separately. If prohibited items or persons with suspicious behavior are found on vehicles or ships, they may be detained at any time and handed over to the local office for transfer to the headquarters for interrogation. (2) All inspectors will receive their original salaries, but will be given a night snack allowance for the evening. Those who have made outstanding contributions to solving major cases or who have been found to be shielding malfeasance by the responsible officers or reported by others will be rewarded or punished accordingly.

Wuxi 78

Opposition to the Establishment of a Nitric Acid Plant: Shiyong Town in the 14th district of the county is surrounded by mountains on the west, north, and south, separated by a giant river, commonly known as Shanmenkou, with excellent terrain. In 1920, the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs sent personnel to survey the Shanwan and establish a Hengchun. Due to an incident it was halted. Last month, the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs planned to open a nitrate plant and sent personnel to survey the mountain again. The mountain is near Taihu Lake, and although the bay is remote, transportation is convenient. It was decided to set up a factory in Tanwan.

Upon hearing this news, Zhang Juchu, Shao Shutang, and more than 60 other citizens of the area, because there are more than 300 households in the village and dense populations in the neighboring villages and alleys, and the mountains are densely populated with tombs, with about 20,000 tombs. If the nitrate plant is realized, the more than 20,000 tombs will be destroyed. Yesterday, they jointly telegraphed the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs, requesting that the nitrate plant be relocated to preserve the tombs and ensure the safety of the ancestors.

Request to Prohibit the Slaughter of Cattle 79

Jin Wanxing, Chen Fuxing, and other cattle slaughtering companies in Xiyi jointly petitioned the central and provincial governments with counterparts from Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Changzhou, Suzhou, and other counties last month, requesting permission to slaughter vegetables cattle to maintain their business. After receiving the petition, the provincial government considered that cattle are of great importance to agriculture, and it is difficult to distinguish between cattle and vegetable cattle. It specifically ordered the Department of Industry to investigate and report, and before the investigation and report is completed, the slaughter should still be prohibited and no tricks should be allowed. Recently, however, the market is flooded with beef, and the loss of farming cattle in various villages has become increasingly common. Therefore, the village chiefs and district chiefs believe that the private slaughter of farming cattle is strictly prohibited, and the prohibition has not yet been lifted, but the loss of farming cattle is already high. The cattle merchants are using tricks. If the slaughter is allowed, the impact on agriculture will be even greater. Yesterday, they petitioned the county to request a prohibition on the slaughter to maintain agricultural production.

The promotion and collection fee was 45 cents per 100 yuan. The district clerks were not allowed to collect the promotion and collection fee again. Ningbo

Reasons for the Deficit of the American Ball Factory 97

Zhao Yuchun, the owner of the American Ball Knitting Factory at Shizhu Bridge in the city of the two ports, started the factory with only 4,000 yuan of capital in the fifth year of the Republic of China. Later, because Mr. Zhao was diligent and hardworking in management, he gradually added new machines and expanded the factory buildings. The number of workers increased to more than a thousand. Now, it has almost become one of the largest factories in Yibu. The financial industry, seeing the factory's large scale, had successively extended loans to Mr. Zhao. Zhao then used these funds to develop business in various places, such as the wholesale outlets in Hankou, and the Rusheng Factory in Lujiabu, etc. Unexpectedly, due to the unstable situation and excessive inventory, all the branches and sub-factories suffered huge losses. Accumulated to date, the debt owed has reached more than 600,000 yuan. The financial industry yesterday convened a meeting of all creditors of the factory at the industry guild hall to discuss the results. Before a maintenance plan is available, two creditor representatives will be appointed to monitor the factory starting today (the 17th) and temporarily suspend incoming goods. According to the person in charge of the factory, the reason for the current funding problems is that the losses of the branch factories and outlets were too great, resulting in a strain on the entire factory. Upon investigation, the total current inventory of the factory is 200,000 yuan, accounts receivable in the Yangtze River area are 100,000 yuan, production machinery is valued at 150,000 yuan, the Hankou wholesale outlet has an inventory of 130,000 yuan, and all the production equipment of the Jiangdong Dyeing Factory is valued at 20,000 yuan. The factory building is worth 20,000 yuan, totaling more than 600,000 yuan, which is sufficient to offset the losses. If the financial industry provides maintenance, there is hope for restoring the original state.

Ministry of Education Promulgates Curriculum Standards for Kindergartens and Elementary Schools (1) 100

Curriculum Standards for Kindergartens and Elementary Schools

Drafting Process

The curriculum standards for kindergartens and elementary schools were drafted by the Ministry of Education, which appointed experts and organized a committee to take charge. The process lasted from October of the 17th year to October of the 21st year, going through the following four stages before completion:

First Stage: Drafting and Compilation. The Ministry of Education appointed various experts and organized a drafting committee for curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools. Starting in October of the 17th year, those with expertise in various subjects of kindergartens and elementary schools were assigned to be responsible for drafting, compiling, reviewing, and revising. By August of the 18th year, the drafting and compilation were completed. The Ministry of Education ordered the provinces and cities to use them as temporary standards for trial implementation. The following gentlemen contributed to the work during this period...

Temporary Standards for Kindergarten Curriculum (in order of number of strokes in surname)

Gan Mengdan, Wu Yanren, Jin Haiguan, Hu Shuyi, Yu Ziyi, Ma Ketan, Zhang Zonglin, Chen Heqin, Ge Liting, Yang Baokang, Jiang Xicen. Temporary Standards for Elementary School Curriculum

(Chinese Language) Wu Yanren, Shi Renfu, Sun Shiqing, Chen Feixia, Zhao Yuren. (Social Studies) Ren Xuanjun, Wu Yanren, Jin Haiguan, Ji Yujiu, Hu Shuyi, Hu Xuanming, Ma Ketan, Sheng Langxi, Zhao Shifa. (Natural Science) Wang Yingruo, Zhu Zheng Yang, Wu Yanren, Li Dingfu, Jin Runqing, Hu Xuanming, Ma Ketan, Xu Yunzhao, Zhang Yahuan, Zhao Shifa, Pan Pingzhi, Jiang Xicen. (Arithmetic) Shen Baiying, Jin Zhusun, Yu Ziyi, Yang Jia Chun. (Work) Wang Huaguo, Yin Bocheng, Wu Yanren, Zhou Shangzhi, Xiong Gao. (Fine Arts) Zong Lianghuan, Xu Mulan. (Physical Education) Zhu Shifang, Wu Rui, Shen Shoujin, Sun Zhenghe, Yang Binru. (Music) He Mingzhai, Wu Yanren, Cheng Maojun, Chen Yupan, Gu Xilin. (Those who participated in all opinions) Zhu Jingnong, Jiang Jing Shuang, Wu Yanren, Shen Baiying, Jin Haiguan, Zhou Shangzhi, Yu Ziyi, Hu Shuyi, Shi Renfu, Ma Ketan, Zhang Zonglin, Gao Junshan, Cao Shouyi, Sun Shiqing, Lei Zhenqing, Yang Jia Chun, Zhang Zonghai. Second Stage: Trial and Research. The Ministry of Education instructed the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to organize research societies and designate schools to conduct trials and research, setting a deadline of June of the 19th year to submit opinions to the Ministry for reference. Subsequently, various provinces and cities followed the order for trial research. However, by July of the 19th year, no opinions had been submitted to the Ministry by the provinces and cities, and there were requests to extend the trial research period. Consequently, the Ministry issued a general order to extend the trial research period for one year, setting a deadline of June of the 20th year to submit the results to the Ministry for record. By June of the 20th year, the results of the trial research were reported to the Ministry by the following regions: Zhejiang Provincial Education Department, Jiangsu Provincial Education Department, Nanjing Municipal Education Bureau, Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, Guangdong Provincial Education Department, Rehe Provincial Education Department, Education Bureau of Huadian County, Jilin Province. In addition, various experimental elementary schools in Jiangsu Province also submitted many opinions. The Zhejiang Provincial Education Department also submitted detailed reports of the trial results of its affiliated schools, with numerous opinions.

Third Stage: Revision and Correction. [Since] it was necessary to change the original drafting committee for curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools, the Ministry of Education appointed experts in the 20th year to reorganize it into a committee for drafting curriculum and equipment standards for primary and secondary schools. It was engaged in collecting opinions from all parties, studying and revising. It was estimated that from June 18th, there were two days of meetings and preliminary review and revision committees. The standards for kindergartens and elementary schools were largely determined, and the unfinished work was assigned to various personnel. On September 20th and 21st, there were two more days of general meetings and review meetings. Various standards were discussed and decided, and handed over to the standing committee for consolidation. The following committee members were scheduled to do their best in this period: Wang Jinxin, Jiang Jing Shuang, Zhu Wenshu, Zhu Baoqin, Wu Yanren, Shen Baiying, Shen Leilian, Li Qingsong, Li Xiaonong, Yi Ke, Lin Duanfu, Hu Shuyi, Hu Yanli, Shi Renfu, Yu Ziyi, Ma Ketan, Ni Zhuhua, Xu Yiqiao, Weng Zhida, Chen Heqin, Zhang Guoren, Peng Baichuan, Zhao Naichuan, Zhao Tingwei, Jiang Xicen, Zheng Hesheng, Xue Dahan, Dai Yingguan, Xie Shuying, Wei Bingxin, Luo Dixian, Gu Shusen. In addition, the following gentlemen participated in the discussion of research issues for various subjects: (Social Studies) Zhao Zhengduo, Jiang Ziqi, (Music) Wang Yungong, Tang Xueyong, Xiao Youmei.

The revision of the standards this time, except for the kindergarten curriculum standards, which have very few changes, the differences between the elementary school curriculum standards and the temporary standards are summarized as follows:

(1) [Party Doctrine] is not set up as a separate subject, and the Party Doctrine teaching materials are fully integrated into the subjects of [Chinese Language], [Social Studies], and [Natural Science]. (2) The hygiene part of the [Social Studies] and [Natural Science] subjects of the temporary standards is separated, and a separate [Hygiene] subject curriculum standard is formulated. (3) The [Work] subject is changed to [Labor], and the commercial information part is deleted, and the commercial information valuation operation is incorporated into the [Arithmetic] and other subjects. (4) [Citizenship] teaching materials are added to the [Social Studies] subject and [the content is revised]. (5) The contents and wording of each subject have been revised. (6) A separate [general outline] is set to be the crown of each subject standard.

Fourth Stage: Compilation Completed 101

After the revision and correction in the third phase, it could have been promulgated, but unfortunately, the Minister and Vice Minister had not completed the review. Then the September 18th Incident occurred, and the standards had to be temporarily put aside. This year, after Minister Zhu arrived at the Ministry, he felt that the curriculum standards were important and needed to be reorganized and compiled. Therefore, he re-appointed members to review and revise them. From August 1st to August 5th, there were five general meetings in total, and the standards were compiled. Later, Minister Zhu felt that the elementary school Chinese curriculum standards were especially important, so he hired literary experts to review them in detail. From September 26th, there were two days of meetings to further refine the elementary school Chinese curriculum standards (the distribution table of teaching materials was drafted during this review). The elementary school civics training standards only had one case for reform during the general meeting in August. After sorting, it was distributed to various committee members for review. On October 6th, the committee members in Beijing were gathered to hold a meeting for discussion. There were two days of meetings, and the standards were largely completed. The following gentlemen contributed to the work during this period:

(Those who participated in all curriculum standards) Wang Jinxin, Wu Yanren, Gu Qingsong, Yi Kezhong, Hu Liyan, Hu Shuyi, Shi Renfu, Xu Suen, Ma Ketan, Chen Heqin, Jiang Xicen, Xue Tianhan, Gu Shusen. (Those who reviewed the elementary school Chinese curriculum standards) Zhou Yutong, Xia Zeng, Zhao Jingshen, Gu Junzheng, Gu Shusen. (Those who participated in the elementary school civics training standards) (In addition to the committee members in Beijing) Wang Wan, Shen Zishan.

The differences between the standards this time and the previous ones are:

1. An increase in civics training standards, which are the standards for moral education in elementary schools. Because elementary schools do not have separate subjects for civics or self-cultivation, etc., regarding moral training subjects, this standard is added as the basis for civics training.

2. The deletion of the minimum graduation requirements. Because some of the original minimum graduation requirements were not specific, and some were too subjective, it was advocated to temporarily delete them. In the future, after the development of standard testing or a performance chart, more objective limits will be set separately. After the completion of the payment standard, it will be sent to the Minister for review, and the Minister and Vice Minister will carefully modify it once. Although it cannot be said that it is without flaws, it was drafted and revised by more than one hundred people, tested and researched in various parts of the country, and took four years. It was only completed after research and discussion by many committee members. It can also be regarded as the most important work in the field of elementary education in recent years. However, the curriculum should be continuously improved. It is hoped that the education community across the country will study together with a view to re-compiling a more complete curriculum standard after several years of implementation. Standing Committee of the Curriculum and Equipment Standards Compilation Committee of the Ministry of Education for Primary and Secondary Schools, recorded on 21.10.20.

Implementation Measures for Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum Standards 102

1. After the promulgation of these standards, all elementary schools in the country should immediately follow them for implementation. However, experimental elementary schools approved by the Ministry of Education or those that have been approved by the competent educational administrative organs due to special local circumstances may make appropriate changes in implementation.

2. If local areas have any opinions on these standards, they should report them to the Ministry of Education at any time as reference material for revision.

3. If the implementation of these standards in various provinces is hampered due to a lack of teachers, the teacher training education should be improved immediately, and the existing elementary school teachers should be given opportunities for further study and research. For example: (1) During vacations or evening spare time, the local educational administrative organs should convene teachers from various schools who are responsible for a certain subject to provide them with basic knowledge and skills about a certain subject and teach them teaching methods. (2) Elementary school teachers should organize research groups on a certain subject to study and practice the knowledge, war, and skills of a certain subject.

4. After the promulgation of these standards, the Ministry of Education will designate several provinces and municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan and the Education Bureau to first invite experts and field researchers to organize a curriculum revision committee. Based on these standards, the operation items for each subject and each academic year will be compiled into specific teaching material outlines, and the achievement limits for each academic year will be attached. After the teaching examples are submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval, they will be implemented in the province and city, and the Ministry of Education will order the provinces and cities to study these examples and compile specific courses for submission to the Ministry of Education for record and implementation.

5. After the promulgation of these standards, the local educational bureaus and departments of various counties and cities will organize local teaching material collection committees in order to supplement local teaching materials. Based on these standards, the operation items of each subject will collect local practical rural teaching materials as supplementary teaching materials and submit them to the competent educational administrative organs for review. After verification, it is added to the specific teaching material outline.

6. The operation items of each subject and each school year of these standards are all arranged using the [setting method], so they often take the subject as the foundation and form a self-contained system. The curriculum is compiled. Please edit the courses according to the season and the psychological arrangement method and organize the necessary teaching materials into mutually connected units. 7. The curriculum should be compiled by each province and city in accordance with the [nature] contained in the standard to determine the complete and simple two types or more than two, so that schools in cities and villages or schools that are well-run and not well-run can follow it.

7. The curriculum of overseas Chinese elementary schools in Nanyang and other places should be compiled separately by local overseas Chinese education administrators and orchid overseas Chinese education associations and orchid overseas Chinese school representatives based on these standards and local conditions, and submitted to the Ministry of Education for review and record (to be continued).

Fellow Villagers from Shaanxi in Beijing Request Zhou Xuechang Not to Be the Head of the Shaanxi Education Department 103

Local News

The Private School Federation of the French Concession Petitioned the Tax-Paying Chinese Association Yesterday 104

Cheng Zhusun Replied, Promising to Convey the Message

Continue to Petition Each Chinese Director Today

The Private Primary and Secondary School Federation of the French Concession, in order to request subsidies from the French Municipal Council, sent representatives from the Standing Committee of the Federation, including Ma Jiazhen, Hong Guang, and Mao Zhaorong, to the Tax-Paying Chinese Association of the French Concession at 2:00 PM yesterday to petition. Cheng Zhusun, the chairman of the association, met them and hosted them. Ma Jiazhen, as a representative, reported the hardships of the education sector in the French Concession being unable to develop and the rights that the tax-paying Chinese Association should enjoy. He requested that the French Municipal Council be asked to allocate 20% of the annual income to Chinese education within the concession and requested subsidies. Cheng then replied that the organization of the association was originally to seek the welfare of the citizens within the concession. He expressed his deep sympathy for the movement made by the gentlemen for the Chinese education sector within the concession and expressed his willingness to assist them. In addition to forwarding the letter to the Municipal Council within three days, he will also send a letter to each Chinese director to jointly strive for the purpose to fulfill the wishes of the gentlemen and it is also the common duty of the citizens within the concession. The representatives then bid farewell and returned. Subsequently, Sun Jiazhen of the Standing Committee of the Association told a Shanghai News reporter that the association's request for the French Municipal Council to subsidize private schools this time was not just for the sake of each private school, but rather to stand on the standpoint of citizens and strive for the rights that citizens should enjoy from the French Municipal Council. Therefore, this work will never be delayed and will continue to seek a larger movement and will never stop until the goal is achieved. The reply from the Tax-Paying Chinese Association today is still satisfactory. It is now scheduled to petition Du Yuesheng and other Chinese directors again at 2:00 PM tomorrow. In addition to submitting a petition to the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Education Bureau to request their efforts, it will also send a letter to the Citizens' Union of the French Concession to provide assistance. The citizens within the concession are indignant and indignant about this matter and have decided to be the backing of the association to achieve the final goal.

Sports

Next Year's National Games 111

Total Budget of More Than 93,000 Yuan

The Organizational Regulations of the Preparatory Committee are Approved

The National Games, which will be held at the Central Sports Ground in the capital on Double Ten Day tomorrow, have had their budget and organizational regulations for the Preparatory Committee approved by the Executive Yuan meeting on the 15th. The total budget has been determined to be more than 93,000 yuan. The list of members of the Preparatory Committee will be decided by the standing meeting of the Ministry of Education's Sports Committee on the 25th of this month, and then the Ministry of Education will send letters of appointment. The Central Sports Ground must be received and the Preparatory Committee for the National Games must be established and instructed by the National Government for the Preparatory Committee for the National Games in the 20th year of the Republic of China before it can be formally received. The organizational regulations of the Preparatory Committee for the National Games next year as resolved by the Executive Yuan are as follows:

▲Organizational Regulations of the Preparatory Committee for the National Games in the 22nd Year Article 1 The name of this meeting shall be the Preparatory Committee for the National Games in the 22nd Year. Article 2 The members of this meeting shall be fifteen to twenty-one, and shall be appointed by the Ministry of Education. Article 3 The meeting year of this meeting shall be set up in the Central Sports Field in the capital. Article 4 The duties of this meeting are as follows: 1. The meeting receives and manages the Central Sports Field by the Preparatory Committee of the Sports College. 2. Preparing for all matters related to the meeting. 3. Handling all matters related to the meeting hall during the meeting. 4. Handling the conclusion report after the meeting. Article 5 There shall be three standing committee members of this meeting, appointed by the Minister of Education from among the committee members to handle daily affairs and convene meetings. Article 6 This meeting shall have a secretary-general who shall handle all affairs of this meeting under the order of the committee. Article 7 This meeting shall have five groups: General Affairs, Engineering, Regulations, Competition, and Reception. Each group shall have one director and several staff members, whose duties are as follows: 1. The General Affairs Group shall handle matters relating to documents, general affairs, accounting, and matters not belonging to other groups. 2. The Engineering Group shall handle construction, layout, decoration, and site design matters. 3. The Regulations Group shall handle the drafting of various regulations and rules of this meeting. 4. The Competition Group shall handle competition order, sports equipment, and convene registration judges and prizes. 5. The Reception Group shall handle the registration of athletes, reception, security, health, fire protection, receipt and distribution of tickets, and other matters. Article 8 Each group may be divided into sections to handle affairs according to the complexity of the affairs. Article 9 This meeting may establish various specialized committees when necessary. Article 10 The meeting's office and various detailed rules shall be formulated separately. Article 11 The Secretary-General may convene meetings of the heads and staff of each group when necessary. Article 12 These Regulations may be amended by the Ministry of Education if there are any matters not covered. Article 13 These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

China Athletic Association Prepares for the International Race 112

Furthermore, the new rules for women's basketball have already been announced. However, for the sake of clarity for all teams, they are re-announced as follows. Please pay attention: ㈠ The radius of the free-throw circle is three feet (originally two feet). ㈡ When holding the ball during a free throw, waiting for more than ten seconds will be considered a violation (previously, it was a technical foul). ㈢ Legal defense is not limited to a vertical plane, as long as there is no body contact or other technical or personal foul. ㈣ During a two-man jump ball, the jumpers should each stand in the semicircle closer to their own basket (i.e., facing away from their own basket) for the jump ball. ㈤ All successful shots are worth two points. ㈥ If a player is fouled while shooting, and the shot is successful, it will be counted as valid, and the player will be awarded one free throw. If the shot is unsuccessful, the player will be awarded two free throws.

Xiqing Basketball Opening Tournament: Xiaguang Wins Over U.S. Navy 120

丨50 to 31丨

Group B: Muer Wins Over Junior High 67 to 19

丨Three Games Tonight丨

The Xiqing Basketball Association opened its tournament last night. Due to a change in the order, only five games were played in Group A. Xiaguang defeated the U.S. Navy's Los Angeles Destroyer by a score of 50 to 31. In Group B, Muer (MM) won over Junior High by a score of 67 to 19. The first half ended with a score of 32 to 14 in favor of Xiaguang. The course of Xiaguang's victory is as follows:

▲ The game was dull at the beginning. In the first half, the U.S. Navy's center, Russell, scored two consecutive shots, and Guan An made one free throw. The Navy took an early lead of 4 to 1. Xiaguang worked hard to catch up and took the lead with a score of 5 to 4. Then the two teams were evenly matched, tying three times. The game was dull because neither side made much progress. Xiaguang's teamwork was lacking, and they relied on individual efforts, which were not very effective. The Navy's shooting was inaccurate, and they ran around without much to show for it. This situation did not change until the score was tied at 10 to 10, when the game finally opened up and showed new developments.

▲ Starting to work together and take the initiative, the effectiveness greatly increased. The three forwards, flowing smoothly, successively scored into the net with ease. The playing style became more organized. They scored 23 points in a row. Looking back at the Navy's performance, it declined rapidly and was beyond repair. Even with repeated substitutions, they did not add a single point. The first half ended with a score of 33 to 10. The situation in the second half remained the same. Although the Navy showed some improvement, it was not enough to change the overall outcome. Xiaguang, having been too aggressive in the first half, gradually showed signs of fatigue, giving the Navy few opportunities to score. The final score was 50 to 31. ▲ The Navy's second-string team's second half was the most exciting part of the game and was also Xiaguang's most triumphant moment. Their teamwork was so smooth that every shot was accurate, which was very impressive. Xiaguang's great victory was somewhat aided by luck. As for the Navy, although they were physically strong, their skills seemed rusty, and their movements were fast but their aim was poor. Their shooting lacked accuracy, and their coordination was often chaotic. They were really just a second-rate team.

Donghua Defeats St. John's Four to Zero 121

Donghua Attacks Without Being Pushy

St. John's Has a Good Fighting Spirit

Donghua played a friendly match with the St. John's University team yesterday at the St. John's field. The crowd was huge, with about 3,000 spectators. The soccer fans in western Shanghai were in for a real treat. Donghua's lineup changed dramatically yesterday. Li Yichen and a strong center back were moved to defense. Li Yichen filled in for You Yichen. Feng Yunyou accompanied the team but did not play. In the second half, Li Ning also took on a managerial role. Yang Renwei returned to the right wing and performed well, which was definitely better than his previous position as a midfielder. Right-back Yin Zhengda also had few weaknesses and made few mistakes, and he was more agile than in the match against the British Navy. On the St. John's side, Wu Youliang led the team, running and assisting without any flaws. Center forward Pang Panfang, right forward Luo Chunren, and inside midfielders Chen and Wu were all promising talents. Overall, St. John's fighting spirit was really good, but unfortunately, their forwards were too slow, and they repeatedly missed good opportunities. Otherwise, they would not have been completely defeated.

Li Silian blew the whistle, and the two teams began a fierce battle. After dozens of exchanges, it was hard to tell who was ahead. Li Yichen saved the ball from a chaotic situation and passed it to Yang Zuo Waner. After some exchanging, he passed to Hong Guang, who dribbled into the penalty area and scored a goal. After St. John's conceded a goal, they launched a major counterattack. Wu Youliang commanded the game, and the whole team worked hard. Pang Panfang made a deep solo run, but he was too far from the goal and had to retreat. He fell down. Pang shot at the goal, but the ball bounced back off the post. The goal was saved. During a chaotic moment, Tu Kaiyuan made a long pass, which Wu Youlin received. Cao Qiuting escaped, bypassed the dragon, and went to intercept the ball. Youlin was unable to dribble. Cao got the ball and shot directly at the goal, scoring another goal. Shortly after, it was lemon time, and they took a group photo to show their camaraderie. When the game resumed, St. John's forwards attacked aggressively several times, but they all failed. Soon, Li Ning made a long drive. Hong Guang dribbled the ball quickly, but he was blocked by Lin Ri. He made a short pass to Renwei, who went to the end line. He was forced into a corner kick by Youlin. Yang Renwei took the kick. The ball fell precisely, only a short distance from the goal. Chen Jiaqiu stepped up and scored another goal. Later, Chen Hongguang scored another goal, and the game ended. ▲ Donghua Team

Middle School Sports Association Football Tournament Scheduled to Begin 123

Divided into [Up] and [Sea] Groups

Tournament Begins on the 23rd of This Month

The attending committee members were Jiang Jingnan (Chairman), Liang Guocai, and Zhang Xi'en. The resolutions of various cases are recorded separately below: ㈠ Tournament Dates: The tournament will begin on the 23rd of this month and end on December 14th. Games will be held at 3:00 PM every Wednesday at various schools. Teams that do not appear within 15 minutes of the scheduled start time will be considered to have forfeited the game (this does not apply if delayed by automobile accident).

㈡ Group Divisions: Schools are divided into the [Up] and [Sea] groups. The [Up] group includes Fushi, Fu Middle, and Zhizhi four schools.

㈢ Tournament System: Each group will adopt a single round-robin system. The winner will receive two points, and the loser will receive zero points. In the event of a draw, each team will receive one point. The teams with the most points in each group will then compete in a final to determine the champion. ㈣ Tournament Rules: The tournament rules will be based on the football rules set by the National Games. However, the game time will be 78 minutes (35 minutes for each half), with a 10-minute break. ㈤ Referees: The home team will hire the referees, subject to the approval of the visiting team. The linesmen will be nominated by each side. The East District Elementary School's Playground 127

The director of the Chinese Education Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council suggested purchasing 3 mu, 6 fen, and 5 li of land near the New East District Elementary School to increase the playground. The Education Committee discussed it, and the Commissioner of Public Works stated that the school and the neighboring Nie Zhongcheng Public School already occupied more than 25 mu of land. Since the land price was too expensive and the school was not a boarding school, there was no need to expand the area any further. The fence built by the contractor would be removed after the work was completed, so the playground would not be divided. The Acting Superintendent of Schools also believed that the existing playground area was sufficient for the needs of both schools and should be jointly used by them through consultation. The committee approved this proposal, and the board of directors approved it as well.

Free Talk

Wu Middle School Girls Raise Winter Clothing 128

— Yan Bōguāng

丨For the Brave Soldiers in the Northeast丨

With their own conscience, the compatriots in Jiangnan must also think about the brave soldiers in the Northeast who are fighting desperately! In the piercingly cold winter, we always ask our friends, "Are you cold?" But are the brave soldiers in the Northeast, who are in the freezing weather, cold? The country belongs to all our compatriots. The brave soldiers are fighting for the country, which means they are fighting for the status of all our compatriots.

The male and female students of various schools in Suzhou, with their own consciences, spent their precious time studying, and spread out in various directions to earnestly solicit donations. The girls' performance was very good. There were traces of the girls in various key areas, various institutions, and various households. Their efforts to solicit donations are worthy of people's praise! With earnest words and a sincere heart, they described the hardships and courage of the brave soldiers in the Northeast, which moved people. Compatriots! If you are not generous in donating, you may have a heart of stone!

Yesterday, I went to Guanqian for something. From Yangyu Lane to Cufang Bridge, I donated more than 20 cents for the brave soldiers back and forth. Every time the car passed in front of the students, it was stopped and donated two cents. When I got out of the car at Yangyu Lane, I saw the driver voluntarily donated two cents of his hard-earned money.

Alas! What an admirable driver!

I wish the sisters and brothers in the amusement field! And the compatriots with ample money! Spend a few cents as you wish! Do not destroy your conscience.

Elephant 129

— Qǐwò

It is said that there was a story that vaguely symbolizes the characteristics of the nation... Once, representatives from various countries gathered together and each wrote an article about elephants. The British title was "Elephant Hunting under British Rule," the French title was "The Elephant and His Lover," the German title was "Introduction to Elephantology," the Polish title was "Elephants and the Polish Question," and the American title was "How to Hunt Big and Good Elephants." The Russian title was "Do Elephants Exist in the World?" I think if there were representatives from Great China attending this gathering, his title would probably be "How to Resist Elephants?" Otherwise, he might write a "Fighting Elephants" article!

Do not be stingy and refuse to donate a cent, and know that you are also a member of the country.

A 109-Year-Old Man 130

— Zhègēn

丨Beard Three Feet Long, Sweeping the Ground When Sitting, Passing the Knees When Standing丨

There are very few long-lived people in China these days. A man named Ruan from Penglai County, Shandong, who is now in the three northeastern provinces, said that he is 148 years old. There is also a man named Li who is over 100 years old. His portrait has been published in various newspapers. Now there is another elderly man, Zhang Zaifeng, who is from Yingzhou, northern Anhui, and is 109 years old. He was born in the Jia Shen year of the Daoguang reign of the Qing Dynasty. He has an extraordinary appearance that is astonishing. The beard on his chin is visible at the root, more than three feet long, and when sitting on a chair, the beard sweeps the ground, which is twice as long as that of Marquis Shou of the Han Dynasty. According to him, after eating immortal peaches, his face became younger, and his beard grew wildly. After carefully inquiring about his secret to longevity, it is nothing more than having few desires and a pure heart. During the Red Sheep Tribulation, he met an immortal who taught him the method of refining elixirs and collecting herbs, which is why he has such longevity.

He cultivated himself in Little Lotus Mountain, but was disturbed by the communists and could no longer live there, so he returned to his hometown. His relatives and old friends have all died, so he had to live in the home of a gentleman surnamed Li. Through the introduction of a friend, he came to Shanghai specifically to form a relationship with a group of pious men and women. He will meet with you in the Great World in a few days.

An Offensive Against Love Films 131

— Cheng Da

In recent years, the development of the film industry, both Chinese and foreign, has truly progressed at a tremendous pace. However, among the large number of productions, it is rare to find a film that does not talk about love, which shows the needs of today's society. At the same time, it occurs to me that there must be many young people whose will has been corrupted, indirectly influenced by these love films.

Young people talking about love is an inevitable psychological trend and a normal phenomenon. However, their pursuit is often based on improper means and blind understanding, resulting in tragedies in society, creating an atmosphere where the country and friends can be forsaken, but not the lover.

In many universities, these facts are especially visible: meeting today and talking about love tomorrow.

If the other party is beautiful and behaves romantically, it can create a lot of jokes, with many hues and colors.

The other day, I watched the new film "Adorable Enemies" by Star Film Company, which gave me a great feeling. The plot of this film briefly describes how college student Xu Yuanlu fell in love with a romantic female classmate, resulting in breaking off relations with his friend Zhao Youcheng. However, Zhao Youcheng spared no sacrifice to persuade him, and [reason overcame emotion], finally awakening Xu Yuanlu.

This film, on the one hand, indicates that friendship is the most precious, and on the other hand, it corrects the concept of love for ordinary college students. In today's market saturated with love films, it is undoubtedly a valuable contribution to suddenly discover such a production that attacks all boring love films.

Brief News 132

— Master Huifeixuan

Pulmonary tuberculosis with hemoptysis is the most difficult disease to diagnose and treat. It has been rumored for a long time at the Chunming Pharmaceutical School on Xueshi Street in Suzhou. The owner, Mr. Huang, had an ancestor who, during the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom era, fled to other places. He met a Mr. Tang who was poor and sick with no place to go. Mr. Huang took pity on him and allowed him to live in a corner, treating him like family. After things calmed down and he returned to Suzhou, Mr. Tang still followed him and eventually died of old age. Before his death, he passed on a secret recipe to Mr. Huang.

Crossroads of Death ㈩㈦ 134

— Fan Yanqiao

Five Also Has a Love Character

On the Jiangmian River in Xiaguan, the Japanese warships anchored there fired several blank shots for no reason, presenting a terrifying phenomenon. The most laughable and contradictory fact was that some people living in Xiaguan were taking their old and young and running to the city in a panic, while at the same time, some people living in the city were carrying boxes and bedding and running out of the city. Han Muliang received the bad news from the ×× department the earliest, so he left the fastest and had already resolved to jump on the train and return directly to his old home in Suzhou before finally stopping to catch his breath.

What he regretted was not the shattering of his rice bowl, but the departure of his vase. He was expressing his feelings to a female comrade and had not yet reached fruition when he was disrupted by the blank shots.

The terror in Xiaguan flowed eastward, and the tension in Shanghai surged westward, converging in the human paradise of Suzhou. The timidity of Suzhou people, like the braised pork of Lu Gaojian, is famous far and wide. Moreover, this invasion by Japanese pirates is not comparable to the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95. Planes with the sun emblem come to circle every day. Muliang barely ate a bowl of porridge after the planes went away, and as usual, he lay on the sofa, dazed. The radio continuously reported: "[Several Japanese warships have arrived at the Huishan Wharf, fully loaded with Japanese soldiers and officers.]" His relatives and friends came one after another to say:

"[We are leaving.]" Muliang said to his wife:

"[Let's go too.]"

The young mistress Han naturally did not object to leaving, but where to go was a question. Muliang thought that if they were to leave, they had to go to Shanghai. There were robbers in the villages and towns, so the foreign concessions in Shanghai were a protective charm. Therefore, he finally "[took his family and other dependents on a local steamer to Shanghai and sent a telegram to his godfather, asking for a long vacation from the ×× department."

Although the concessions in Shanghai also heard cannon fire every minute or two and saw the red flames in the northern suburbs, and although they saw trucks full of Japanese soldiers speeding across the streets, there were still wire fences and sandbags separating them into another world, where various entertainments and supplies of food and sex were still available. In the autumn of 1894-95, he lived in the concessions, not caring about anything, and went to the Great World at night to guess riddles. Now, guessing riddles is no longer fashionable, and he feels that he has lost a boring pastime. He happened to meet a colleague from the ×× department, who led him to the Parisian Dance Hall when they talked about these days' lives.

At first, he didn't find it very interesting, but after doing a few dances, he gradually became fascinated and went every night. He had no purpose, so he casually pulled a dancer in the dance hall and, with the decadent music, embraced her in the drunken-like lights and danced. The dancers, apart from the differences in the length, fatness, and thinness of their bodies, had bare breasts pressed against you, smooth jade arms pulling you, rounded powder legs resisting you, the fragrance of powder intoxicating you, the dreamy soft words tempting you, and the drowsy starry eyes teasing you. Each had these innate abilities, and it was difficult to distinguish a high or low level. In short, after being intoxicated, the appearance was secondary.

Indian cotton saw a firm market due to buying by speculators and brokers. Equivalent to Pingle rose by 1 rupee, Aumla rose by 0.75 rupees, and White Rose continued to fall by 0.375 rupees. Grain: Large Fall, Small Rebound in Rice Market Downriver 145

▲ Yesterday in South Shanghai, over twenty sources of supplies arrived. Transactions on this street were lighter compared to before. Regular Northern Jiangsu and Pingli Zhongguan goods fell by a small amount of 0.2 tael. Early and late rice also saw small price drops. Yangdujian and Bianyin Yuanwei lacked momentum, indicating a downstream trend.

▲ At Xinzha, cargo arrivals down the Suzhou River from inland areas were still strong, numbering around 42 or 43. The situation was in a slump. Regular Changzhou and Jiangyin white rice fell by around 0.2 tael. Luyang was sold as soon as it arrived. The opening set the tone. The six types of "Hundred Brothers" were undifferentiated. Over 2,500 to 2,600 dan of rice were unloaded downriver.

Foreign Merchants Re-Engage in Hunan Rice 146

丨Hunan Rice Slightly Upward in Foreign Markets丨

Yesterday, the market for foreign merchant rice saw 本客 (local merchants?) disinterested. The previous day, no transactions occurred. Market sentiment and confidence were downward. The Fuzhou gang, which had a purchase appetite, saw prices weaken and resumed buying on the market, acquiring 1,600 packages of oil, Jing, and other rice from Hunan. Four hundred packages of foreign rice in small bags were acquired. Hunan rice prices fell 0.1 to 0.2 tael compared to the previous market. Due to sufficient inventory and ongoing shipments, cargo owners were eager to sell off at discounted prices, leading to price drops in transactions. Foreign rice, on the other hand, saw little circulating on the market and even fewer resales. Cargo owners had excellent sentiment. The price increase in small bags was slightly larger than the previous day, rising by 0.2 to 0.3 tael. North foreign gangs also casually purchased 500 large bags, with prices remaining at 6.5 yuan. Small bags were priced at 7.8 yuan, Hunan machine-processed oil rice at 8.85 to 8.78 yuan.

Also, machine-processed Jing rice was priced at 8.55 yuan. And, Jing rice was priced at 8 yuan.

Flour Market Stabilized This Month 147

丨All Other Months Consistently Lower丨

Yesterday's flour market saw current flour from Beihua still strong, with a firm market trend. The price for flour from the Navy Yard has already reached 1 tael and 9 qian and 2.5 fen. Unbranded flour was consistently priced higher by 2.5 fen. However, current flour for the current month can still be drawn from the exchange. High-grade flour increased by 6 fen, while medium and second-grade flour increased by 4 to 2 fen. Currently, the northern rivers have not yet frozen, so the purchasing appetite is good and the market still shows promising signs. Futures prices declined across the board due to continuous firm orders for foreign wheat, with two ships scheduled to load on December 5th, and another ship of loose cargo loading immediately. Prices were 3 taels 4 qian 8 fen, 3 taels 5 qian 3 fen, and 3 taels 5 qian 6 fen. After Fufeng and other companies secured their orders, they immediately shorted the market, causing a consistent decline. However, the current month's price remains stable due to current flour availability. The closing price for the current month is still large at 0.075 tael, next month is small at 0.0125 tael, January is small at 0.015 tael, February is small at 0.01 tael, March is small at 0.0125 tael, and April is small at 0.01 tael, it is said.

Wheat Market: Futures Weak, Spot Firm 148

Yesterday's wheat market saw near-term and long-term prices decline consistently after opening in the morning and afternoon. Due to the small number of foreign wheat merchants and three more ships of Australian wheat being traded, prices also fell by a small amount of 0.03 to 0.04 tael. Sentiment was soft. Factories shorted flour futures, while traders and speculators shorted wheat futures. Therefore, prices for each month declined after the opening. The afternoon saw further weakness. The closing price for November was small, down 0.03 tael, December was not open, January fell by 0.06 tael, February was small, March was small, and April was small, down 0.04 tael. No current wheat in stock. A total of 200 packages of newly arrived Pinghu wheat were opened on the market at a price of 3 taels 3 qian 8 fen, which is approximately 0.2 tael higher than the previous lowest price.

Sugar Market: Arrival of Large Quantities of Dutch Red Sugar Causes Weakness 150

Yesterday's sugar market saw an increase in the premium and a slight reduction in Dutch sugar, which would normally be expected to lead to an increase in price. However, weak sales from all parties in the past week caused the public association's assessment to decline slightly. No. 24 coarse sugar and ordinary white sugar was initially assessed at 14 taels 8 qian 2.5 fen, then later assessed at 8 qian 1.25 fen, a decrease of 0.025 to 0.0375 tael compared to the previous day. High-grade RA sugar was priced at 14 taels 9 qian 2.5 fen. No. 18 medium-grade white sugar was priced at 14 taels. No. 20 medium-grade white sugar was priced at 14 taels 3 qian due to a lack of goods and no arrivals. Very firm. Due to the recent arrival of over 48,000 packages of No. 8, 9, and 10 Dutch red sugar, there was a sudden feeling of oversupply, and the trend weakened. There is a risk of continued weakening in the future market. The arrival of Jianbing brand goods has recently slightly increased, but sales are not strong, resulting in no large-scale transactions. Yesterday's market saw a total of 0.98 tael of manual ice sugar sold, with some sales, it is said.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms Still Struggling to Advance Silk Sales 151

The New York raw silk market has returned to weakness. Actual sales in Lyon are still sluggish. European and American firms in Shanghai are all considering taking advantage of low prices to stockpile, while factories believe that silk production costs are relatively high and are unwilling to sell at a loss. The market atmosphere is sluggish and quiet.

High Prices for High-Quality Zhenmei Green Tea 152

Yesterday, the tea market for foreign firms in this port saw British firms such as Jardine Matheson, Ewo, and Xiangfu actively purchasing high-quality Zhenmei green tea from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other areas. Transactions were quite strong. However, due to the market's prolonged sluggishness, Chinese tea merchants' financial strength was particularly weak. Market prices for Zhenmei from Wudong Tunxi have fallen to over 70 taels, another 6 or 7 taels lower than before. As for Zhenmei from Wubei, firms such as Baochang and Tianxiang had some negotiations, but there was no major progress. Transactions for other varieties such as Gongxi pearl tea were also scarce, it is said.

Oil Market: Asphalt and Zhejiang Road Oil Surge 153

The asphalt market in Hubei remains stable, while Zhejiang Road overall reports surging prices. Because Hangzhou stated that the large drop in oil prices and cheap sales have long been exhausted, and new goods have not arrived, various oil merchants were originally low on inventory and prepared to sell. New oil merchants have not acquired new goods and most pressing mills have not yet bought seeds, so they are unwilling to sell. This has caused a slight rise in prices, and asphalt prices have also increased. But this is only due to psychological factors. Merchants see that market prices have already risen, so they refrain from buying, and sales are still slow. Therefore, after the price increase, transactions have become quieter than before the increase, and the market has gradually become flat. It is currently heard that Zhejiang seeds are being actively sold at the origin, but sales have not improved, so there is a fear that the current situation may be difficult to sustain. This port's merchants have limited inventory and often receive mixed-grade oils, so they are unable to actively acquire new goods. Therefore, although Zhejiang oil is reported to be increasing in price, they are indifferent to it.
