Tianlun Silk Weaving Factory Suddenly Suspends Work Yesterday 188

Conflicts Erupt Between Day and Night Shift Workers

The Social Bureau Will Send Personnel to Mediate

The Tianlun Silk Weaving Factory in Mingyuanfang, Huade Road, recently suffered from poor business and switched to using inferior raw materials to reduce costs. However, the workers believed that these raw materials were difficult to spin and weave and demanded subsidies for food expenses. The factory owner refused to comply, resulting in a dispute. The Social Bureau sent Chen [illegible] Shan to mediate, but the matter has not been resolved. Last night, the factory manager, Fang Dehua, suddenly announced the temporary suspension of the night shift, but did not notify any workers to stop working or disperse. Therefore, when they went to work yesterday morning, the day and night shift workers went to work at the same time, and both sides competed for work, resulting in a conflict. Seeing that the labor situation was not good, the factory closed the electric motors, drove the workers out of the factory, and announced a temporary shutdown of all workers. The workers immediately reported to the Silk Weaving Industry Union of the Fourth District. The executive director, Wei Shouchang, filed a petition and went to the Social Bureau with Fang Shaofu and other representatives of the factory workers. Chen Yushan of the Third Section of the Bureau came out to receive them and promised to negotiate with the factory immediately, ordering them to resume work as soon as possible.

Seven Russians Risk Escape from Vladivostok and Arrive in Shanghai 189

Regarding Vladivostok: Recently, seven Russians, disgusted with the communist regime, escaped from Vladivostok on a small gasoline-powered boat. After sailing for fifteen days, they arrived in Shanghai on Tuesday. The boat is named "Sakudo" and is now docked in Pudong, not far from Lujiazui. The reporter (16th) inspected the boat yesterday and saw the traces of storms in the Sea of Japan. The boat belongs to the seven people. Except for the boat owner and the mechanic, who are both around 45 years old, the rest are young people. It is said that they set sail from Vladivostok on the 31st of last month, pretending to be fishing as usual, only taking extra gasoline and food. When they sailed into the sea and escaped the patrol boats of the Russian authorities, they encountered two major storms. A huge amount of seawater poured into the cabin, but the boat was strong and remained safe. The engines did not cause any problems. They then rounded the southern tip of Korea, passed Jeju Island, and went straight to the Yangtze River. They had no nautical charts and relied only on ordinary maps to navigate. After entering the Wusongkou, they were inspected by customs and were allowed to enter the port. On Tuesday night, they sailed to Pudong and docked. The people were very happy to arrive in Shanghai. Their future plans are still undecided, and they urgently hope to find work to make a living. They also hope to sell or rent out the boat. According to them, the situation in Vladivostok this year is worse than last year. Everyone has to work, and no one is spared from hunger and cold. The fish caught by fishermen are bought by the authorities at government-set prices and given receipts. Foreign tourists have special stores that supply foreigners with goods in exchange for money. Overseas Chinese buy goods from these stores and secretly resell them, making huge profits. If they are caught, they can only eat cheap fish and vegetables, and there is no meat. It is said that it is difficult to find any internal goods in Vladivostok.

The Completion of the Four Virtues Hall in Mr. Huang's Villa is a Grand Event 190

Reception for All Sectors Today and Tomorrow

The news that Mr. Huang Jinrong's villa will be open to visitors from all walks of life today and tomorrow has already been reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday, around 11:00 AM, the completion ceremony of the Four Virtues Hall was held, with more than a thousand people attending. They gathered in the hall and performed the ceremony as usual. First, Mr. Huang gave a speech, followed by Mr. Lai Bao, representing Mr. Wang Boling, giving a speech. Finally, Mr. Wang Zhongxian gave a reply on behalf of the students. The ceremony ended at 12:00 PM, followed by a meal together, where they toasted and celebrated in a joyful atmosphere. It was truly a grand gathering on the beach. After the meal, they visited the garden and took a group photo to commemorate the occasion. The full text of the speeches and the Four Virtues Hall inscription are extracted below.

Mr. Huang's Speech: Briefly, "I have served in Shanghai for more than forty years, and I have been fortunate to receive the love and mutual assistance of people from all walks of life. I am fortunate not to have failed. The reason why I have been able to gain a slight position in society is only because of the two principles of hard work and loyalty. Do not seek help from others for things that you can do yourself. Do not leave things that can be completed today for tomorrow. My life has come from hard work. If you treat others with sincerity, they will repay you with sincerity. Although your positions may be different, whether you are in government or in business, the way of dealing with people is the same. If you can discipline yourself with hard work and treat others with sincerity, you will be able to achieve success. I am now sixty-five years old, and although my energy is still strong, I feel that it is not as good as before. Society is becoming increasingly complex. I feel that I am old and incompetent and cannot bear the heavy responsibilities. The country is in a time of great difficulty, and great disasters will come in the future. The heavy responsibilities in the future depend on you young people. I have long wanted to retire, reflect on my mistakes, and return to my original state. Therefore, I built several rooms next to the family shrine and slightly decorated them to relieve my mind and avoid worldly affairs. I am grateful to you for donating to build this hall to commemorate me. It is named 'Four Virtues'. Who am I to dare to admire the sages? I only wish to encourage you to practice the four virtues of literature, conduct, loyalty, and trustworthiness."

Mr. Wang's Speech: "Today, we are participating in the celebration of the completion ceremony, and we are very happy. This is the crystallization of Mr. Jinrong's life's work, and it is worthy of admiration and respect. What I heard from Mr. Jinrong just now can indeed be our guide in dealing with the world, but from an objective point of view, there are many more virtues that he possesses. From my personal point of view, the first is moral sentiment. He treats the world with sincerity, without deception or suspicion, whether they are rich or powerful, or without money or power. He is different from those who are snobbish and opportunistic. This is one. The second is his humble attitude. Mr. Jinrong is always humble in dealing with people, not only to his superiors, but also to his subordinates. He is different from those who fawn on their superiors and are arrogant to their inferiors. This is the second. The third is his equal attitude. He treats everyone equally, regardless of their status. Others make friends by strictly distinguishing social classes. Mr. Jinrong makes friends with everyone, from government officials to laborers, treating them equally. This is the third. The fourth is his compassionate heart. He is always willing to help those who are in need, taking their difficulties as his own. Other good deeds, such as disaster relief, poverty relief, and orphan care, are well known and cannot be fully described. This is the fourth. The fifth is his frugal virtue. People see that his life is already comfortable and luxurious, but he is not like that. He cherishes material resources and is frugal in his self-indulgence. He never throws away half-smoked cigarettes and does not use fine leather for his fur coats. This is the fifth. The sixth is his courageous demeanor. He has served in society and in the French Concession police force for decades, and he has always used his intelligence and courage to solve difficult and dangerous cases. This is the sixth. The seventh is his regular routine. Most people living in Shanghai work day and night and have irregular routines, but Mr. Jinrong, both during and after his work, has never gotten out of bed later than eight o'clock in the morning. He has fixed times for lunch and dinner. I have lived with him for seven or eight years and have never seen him change his routine. This is the seventh. The eighth is his wise vision. His vision is sharp and unparalleled, not even comparable to that of politicians. Moreover, his will is very firm. In the past two or three years, the atmosphere in Shanghai has changed almost constantly, but Mr. Jinrong has always used his sincere heart to support the truth that should be supported. This kind of understanding is truly wise and worthy of our admiration. This is the eighth. Based on the above points, which are only my personal, one-sided understanding, there are many more good qualities that I do not know about, but these few points are enough to make his life a success. I am fortunate to be at the end of the list and to participate in this grand ceremony. I am very happy. These few words cannot express even a fraction of my feelings. I am truly ashamed."

Inscription of the Four Virtues Hall: "Mr. Jinrong, a master of ethics, hails from the Huang clan of Yuyao. His pure and harmonious virtue has been evident since childhood, and his outstanding talent shines brightly in the world. Since residing in Shanghai, he has been encouraging the promotion of norms, emulating Lu Lian in resolving disputes and Lord Mengchang in valuing righteousness. His fame and reputation have spread far and wide. In the spring of Jiazi, he built a family shrine at Jihejing in western Shanghai. He sincerely performs sacrifices to his ancestors to fulfill his filial piety and promote good customs. The empty space next to the shrine violates the principles of feng shui, so he transformed it into a garden with flowing springs and stacked rocks, where beautiful plants grow luxuriantly. In his leisure time, he often rests there with his students, creating a joyful atmosphere like the spring breeze of the Yi River. The master once said: 'Confucius used literature, conduct, loyalty, and trustworthiness to educate his three thousand disciples. I have been reading the Analects since I was young and admire these words. I encourage you to strive for these virtues together.' The students respectfully retreated and reflected on his words. Without literature and conduct, one cannot develop talent; without loyalty and trustworthiness, one cannot achieve virtue. They said, 'Though we are not smart, we will strive to do these things.' Therefore, they raised funds to build a hall in the eastern corner of the garden and named it 'Four Virtues'. Now, the chairman of the National Government, General Chiang Kai-shek, has gladly written a plaque for it. At the time of the completion, the students raised their cups and ascended the hall. They saw the newness of the halls and the permanence of the model. They were delighted and danced, expressing their feelings in words and songs, praising: 'Yinishan established the teachings, with literature, conduct, loyalty, and trustworthiness. Since the style has declined, who will gather the remnants? The master alone holds on to these words and teaches us earnestly. The hall is solemn, and the flowers and bamboo exude their fragrance. Please take this hall as a reminder to strive for the refinement of virtue. O master, master, why not drink first from this brewed wine, enjoying this joy?'"

Wang Nansheng's Suicide Due to Economic Hardship 194

Wang Nansheng, a 32-year-old Tianjin native who ran a shoe store, recently became unemployed and, feeling the pressure of economic hardship, suddenly had the thought of ending his life. On the 15th, around noon, he purchased raw opium. He went to the Fuxing Inn, located at No. 54 An'najin Road, Nanyang Bridge, in the French Concession, rented room number one under the pretext of lodging, and ingested the opium to commit suicide. Around midnight that night, he began to groan in pain as the poison took effect. The tea boy noticed and immediately sent him to Renji Hospital. However, due to the severity of the opium poisoning, treatment was ineffective. He died at 9:45 PM the following evening. The hospital reported the death to the Xiafei Road French Concession Police. Detectives transported the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Hall for an autopsy. As no family members were found, the case was reported to Deng Baosun, a prosecutor from the Second Special Court, the following morning. He arrived at the scene and confirmed that the deceased had committed suicide by poisoning. After the autopsy, the prosecutor returned to the courthouse. According to the report of the detective in charge, the prosecutor questioned Zhang Jiyou, the tea boy of the Fuxing Inn, about the circumstances of the discovery. The prosecutor then ordered that the body be handed over to Tongren Fuyuan Hall for photographs, cleansing, and burial, pending identification by relatives.

Discovery of Fake Goods Sales 201

Huada Music Store, located on the fifth floor of the Continental Emporium in this city, is the distributor of Lion Brand beef and chicken extract from the German Martha Pharmaceutical Factory. It has a very good reputation and is considered a leading tonic, so its business is exceptionally prosperous. Unexpectedly, recently, fake goods have appeared on the market. Three weeks ago, a customer who regularly consumed Lion Brand beef extract brought in a bottle and questioned why the taste had changed recently and the effectiveness was much worse than before. The store staff did not know it was fake, so they exchanged it for a new bottle. That evening, manager Cao Mengdao went to the store and noticed that the counterfeit product had the Chinese characters on the left and the English characters on the right, while the genuine product had the Chinese characters on the left and the English characters on the right. The strokes of the characters were also different and easily identifiable. Last Saturday, they discovered that a certain company had also imported five dozen counterfeit products, with a purchase price much lower than the genuine product. When they inquired with the company, they learned that the seller was Junxiang De Kee Trading Company and produced an invoice. Huada then reported this to the general patrol police station on Simalu (4th Avenue). Since it was a Saturday, the station was not open for official business. On Monday, they requested a search warrant from the court. The police station, along with Russian detective and Chinese detective Zhao Datong, notified Huada to send someone to accompany them to search the Junxiang De Kee Trading Company on Dongqi Grist Street. They found thirteen and a half batches of counterfeit goods. When asked where they came from, they said they were purchased from a certain large pharmacy on 日大馬路 (Rida Malu) [Japanese Great Road] and produced an invoice. The two detectives then went to the pharmacy, which claimed it was purchased from the Zhiwei Pharmacy on 英華街 (Yinghua Street) [English China Street] and also produced an invoice. Upon inspecting the ledger, it showed that they had imported 25 dozen. Then, they went to the Zhiwei Pharmacy for investigation, and only found seven bottles. They asked where the manager was, but the pharmacy claimed that manager Tao Muju had gone to 前途 (Qiántú) to negotiate the beef extract matter. When they went again in the evening, there was an invoice issued by the Shengli Company, showing that they had imported more than 150 dozen, with the address at No. 15 Fuchang Lane, Xixin Bridge. The peddler was Zhang Ruichen, a Ningbo native who was a salesman for the Huasheng Company, which sells Dali Brand beef and chicken extract. The two detectives went to Fuchang Lane, but there was no No. 15. They went to search Zhang Ruichen's home, but Zhang had already fled with his family after hearing the news. The police station believes the Zhiwei Pharmacy is highly suspicious. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated to the court that they were preparing to file a public prosecution. The court approved the request and summoned Tao Muju, manager of the Zhiwei Pharmacy, to court for further investigation. The case was then postponed. It is heard that Huada Pharmacy has suffered enormous losses due to the counterfeiting and has engaged lawyer Yuan Yangan to file a criminal complaint with an attached private prosecution.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Introduction

The Issue of Public Childcare 215

— Ms. Pinglin

The issue of public childcare is the most essential issue for female emancipation and equal opportunity. Because if we don't pay attention to the issue of public childcare, even though women can leave their families and work in society, for women who have given birth, it goes without saying that they must shoulder the responsibility of raising their children at home because they cannot abandon them. Or, as some say, "The calls for women's employment are growing louder every day. Even the wives and daughters of big shots are condescending to serve society... There are female staff members, female section chiefs, female judges, female county magistrates, female secretaries in various departments, female clerks in shops and banks, female hostesses in amusement parks and restaurants, female nurses in hospitals, female teachers and staff in schools, female workers in factories... all these people are taking over the positions of men... At that time, cooking, washing clothes, and taking care of children at home will be the work of men. Otherwise, it will not be too late to promote male employment." Indeed, that is not wrong at all. But we only know that when women work in society, the thousands of years of women taking care of domestic affairs will be handed over to men. Then, wouldn't men be doing women's work and women doing men's work, exchanging like this? I am afraid that in the future, men will also demand the promotion of employment like women do now. In fact, it is not such a cycle.

Because society is composed of human beings, and since women are human beings, and their intelligence and physical strength are not much different from men, why should they depend on men and live a life of slavery? Therefore, women should go to society to support themselves and achieve the principle of gender equality. Men should work hard in society as much as possible and do not need to wash clothes, cook, and take care of children at home. Break the inherent family form and make a living separately (this refers to unmarried women). For women who have given birth, of course, it is impossible. In this situation, we can only advocate public childcare. Where there is public childcare, women who work in society will not be able to raise their children at home, and it will never affect the healthy development of their children! Because to organize public childcare, of course, we need specialists who are good at teaching and raising children to do it. We teach and raise children according to the principle of division of labor, so that children's moral, intellectual, and physical education can develop in parallel, and the effect will definitely be better than the old style of relying solely on the mother for life. With this kind of public childcare organization, women can achieve their true liberation. Although this is the current ideal, the trend of facts will eventually be realized one day. People should no longer hold the bad idea that men are superior to women, purely take individuals as units, men and women should develop in parallel, and work together in various careers. Men do not need to fear that their positions will be taken by women, and there will be a day to promote men's employment.

Climbing the Saoyelou (Sweeping Leaf Tower) 216

— Yi Bingchu

Having seen the vicissitudes of life is this tower, do not record the years in spring and autumn. I only hear the sound of drums and horns filling Zhongshan, and still hear the song of water chestnuts sung by Mo Chou. Drinking and eating as they please, the weak fill the kitchen. Devouring wantonly does not last all morning. The lessons of Yin are clear. The drums of Liaoyang resound in the battle. Struggling to put all one's eggs in one basket, the hot blood flows torrentially.

Science

Research on Sea Sponges 217

— Shunji

……Small Knowledge One……

The nature of sea sponges The other name for sea sponges is haimian, which is a type of sponge animal. They grow at the bottom of the sea, and their roots also grow on the surface of rocks... When the sea sponge is alive, there must be flesh attached to it, like a kind of soft paste... When we cut it off from the water, there is nothing attached to it, only a solid, elastic, and porous skeleton body.

The Life of Sea Sponges The pores in the sea sponge are mostly the mouths of the sea sponge. When water passes through the many crevices of the sea sponge, the food in the water is sent into the small holes, and then the small holes contract; they send the water out again, and when sending the water out, it passes through the large holes in the sea sponge... Food with nourishing nutrients in the water is preserved, and if there is no nourishing food, it is sent out with the water. This is probably the situation of the life of sea sponges at the bottom of the sea.

How to Get Sea Sponges Sea sponges grow at the bottom of the sea, but how do we get them? There is a kind of person who specializes in collecting sea sponges, and we call them sea sponge collectors. They have been practicing collecting sea sponges since they were children. When they want to collect sea sponges, they ride in a small boat to the middle of the sea... They take a large stone and tie it to their feet, tie a rope around their body, surround their neck with a large bag for collecting sea sponges, and hold a long and very sharp knife in their hand. When they are all prepared, they immediately jump into the water and go straight to the bottom of the sea. They begin their work, cutting off... as much as they can cut off, and then put it in the large bag hanging around their neck. After cutting it, they immediately climb up, but when they are at the bottom of the sea, they cannot stay for more than three minutes, because if they stay for more than three minutes, they may drown. We see how terrible the livelihood of sea sponge collectors is! The Use of Sea Sponges Because sea sponges are porous, elastic, soft, and smooth, we use them to wash away the dirty things rotting in the skin, which is their best use.

A Surprise and a Joy Seen in the Advertisement of the Fifth One Newspaper 218

— Qiu Zuo

School Photo

MissCry 219

— Chen Zhou

It seems it's not only Chinese teachers who are like this. As the bold articles published in this journal about their sketches say, English teachers can sometimes be even more ridiculous and pathetic, especially blue-eyed, blonde-haired teachers. MissCry, mentioned in this article, is a good example.

She is a foreigner, a graduate of some second-rate university in the ancient country, and although she already had a fiancé, because both families were poor, they could not marry immediately. She had no choice but to leave her lover and her beloved hometown, cross the Pacific Ocean, and come to this open trading port in East Asia: Shanghai. Relying on her being a foreigner, she was introduced by a friend to work as an English teacher in our school, preparing to earn some money and save up for their wedding expenses. She really deserves to be pitied! But the students couldn't sympathize with her, always messing around and talking nonsense, saying her teaching methods were bad, and her textbooks were bad. In fact, this was all the idea of the head of the English department. She wanted to change the teaching methods and textbooks, but the head of the English department didn't agree. Seeing that she wasn't changing the teaching methods and textbooks, the students completely ignored her in class, letting her ask questions and seek answers, but always ignoring her. She had no choice but to cry, crying in front of the students. Sometimes she got angry and said she wouldn't teach us anymore, so she would leave before the end of class.

But the next day, she still came to class and, with tears in her eyes, urged us not to treat her like this again.

Page 18

Yes, good students, after hearing this, would definitely not treat her like this again, at least thinking of her plight and showing some pity, being quieter in class. But unfortunately, she encountered this kind of student. The more she treated the students this way, the more the students saw her as a pushover, easy to bully. Like this, once, twice, three times... The students made trouble, she cried. She really had no way. Perhaps she was complaining about her bitter fate. Sometimes, when she talked about, or thought about, her

fiancé, she couldn't help but wail and cry. Finally, because she cried, the students gave her the nickname MissCry. In reality, the MissCry I mentioned above is not her real name.

Like this, autumn passed and spring came, and she, who washed her face with tears every day, had lived in our school for two years. After the September 18th Incident in the Northeast, she expressed her sympathy to us, saying, "Children, you are now trying to solve problems that adults cannot solve. I am very willing to help you. If you need me anywhere..." Sure enough, one day, about a few days before Christmas, she asked each of us to write a letter detailing the actual situation of the Japanese invasion of the Northeast, and also writing a request for some help or sympathy for us, and it would be even better if we could boycott Japanese goods! She attached these letters to her New Year's cards sent to friends and relatives in America. She said, "This way, my friends and relatives can understand the truth about this Japanese invasion of the East, and through this, one person can tell ten, ten can tell a hundred... perhaps we can get some small help!" Naturally, although this is trivial, it is also a kind of international propaganda. On this point, I express my respect and gratitude to Miss Cry!

Then, the January 28th Incident broke out, and she went home at that time. It is said that she is now married to her fiancé and living together!

Such a Family

The Heritage of a Pest 220

— Xu Yu

Zhen, whom I hadn't seen for two years, suddenly came as an uninvited guest yesterday. Xiu Mei was delighted to reminisce with her, but she sighed with a frown: "The world is changing, and fortune and misfortune are unpredictable. In these three years, I have experienced family disasters and suffered hardship. If I hadn't acquired these meager knowledge in school back then, relying on teaching to make a living, I would have become a starving corpse by now!"

Xiu Mei asked suspiciously, "Didn't your late father leave a lot of inheritance? Why would you suffer so much?" She said hatefully, "It is precisely because of those many inheritances that I feel endless pain in my spirit. Alas! If my late father could have kindly distributed his wealth and used it for public welfare, instead of leaving behind these pestilent inheritances, then my two wise and promising elder brothers might not have degenerated like this, and my happy family wouldn't have fallen to this point! Speaking of it, it's truly heartbreaking. Before father's bones were cold, my second brother and elder brother started arguing over the property, causing deep-seated opinions.

The reason is that my elder brother has always been a bookkeeper in a money shop in Beiping, with limited monthly income, so after my father died, my mother ordered my elder brother to take care of the family affairs at home, to avoid traveling from afar, since the family had to manage the fields and rent accounts anyway.

Unexpectedly, my second brother suddenly quit his job at the Tianjin Bank for no reason and came home, saying, "Everyone has a share in father's inheritance. Now that elder brother is leisurely at home as a young master, I don't want to hold someone else's rice bowl either, so let's come and manage the family affairs together."

From then on, my elder brother and second brother had to compare everything and make sure everything was the same. For example, if my elder brother made a fox fur coat worth two hundred yuan, my second brother had to make one of the same value, not even one cent less than ninety-nine yuan.

Not only were my elder brother and second brother like this, but my elder sister-in-law and second sister-in-law were also like this. They compared clothes and jewelry piece by piece, and even with trivial things like socks, they haggled over every detail, absolutely unwilling to be careless.

When my father was alive, after each autumn harvest, he would routinely go to the countryside to collect rent. Now my elder brother said, "I'm not used to the desolate life in the countryside," and didn't want to go. My second brother was afraid that if he went, my elder brother would be at home feasting and making merry, so he didn't want to go either.

As a result, they would rather take out money and hire someone else to go, rather let others embezzle, but not let their own compatriots benefit! My elder brother loved to drink brandy the most. With a glass in hand, he didn't care about anything. Although my second brother didn't want him to enjoy the benefits alone, he hated that he couldn't handle alcohol and would get drunk after drinking.

My second brother hated it so much that his teeth itched, saying, "You drink fine wine, and I'll smoke opium." He bought a very exquisite opium smoking set and spent all day indulging in smoke. At first, he just wanted to vent his anger, just smoking for fun, but after smoking for two or three months, he gradually turned pretense into reality and became addicted, unable to stop.

My elder brother certainly wouldn't show weakness, so the two brothers lay side by side, filling the room with black smoke, and finally my elder brother also became addicted to opium.

They turned day into night, reversing morning and evening, and sank into the underworld. Not only did they leave the affairs of the fields and rent to others, but they also didn't care about the shop affairs of the exclusive shares opened at my home, letting those handlers steal and embezzle everything. This year, they even caused the two cloth shops that my parents had painstakingly created to lose two or three hundred thousand yuan and go bankrupt.

The fields and houses had also long been sold by my two "inseparable" elder brothers for consumption. Alas! A good family has now been reduced to such a ruin. Speaking of it, it's so heartbreaking..." Zhen choked up and couldn't continue speaking.

Dead End

Selling Books 221

— Yi

He quickly packed a large bundle of books.

His heart seemed to feel a surge of sadness, feeling that he had really fallen too low; even these books that he usually cherished like his life had to be sent to the used bookstore.

As he ran out of the dormitory with this large bundle of books, the landlady happened to be standing at the door, looking him up and down with some curiosity. He hurriedly lowered his head, didn't greet her, and rushed past.

Walking onto the road, the piercingly cold wind blew on him. He felt extremely cold, and his body trembled. However, he just silently walked, carrying the books. The road was crowded with people, jostling and clamoring. Trams and cars, rickshaws sped past, but it seemed that he had no feelings about any of it. Walking to the entrance of a used bookstore, he saw the sign for buying used books in the dim light. He was just about to go in, but he immediately backed out. He felt that going into a used bookstore to sell books was a shameful, degenerate act. He pulled down his hat and still hesitated at the entrance of the bookstore, hesitating to go in.

"I didn't steal someone else's books to sell. I'm taking my own beloved old books to sell. This is a legitimate and honorable act. What's there to be ashamed of? Go in! To solve my own livelihood problems, I have no choice but to do this. Gather your courage and go in!" He pulled his hat down to his eyebrows and finally walked into the door.

"Sir! What books do you want to buy?"

"No, I have a few old books. Please see if you want them?" He forced himself to say a few words. "How much do you want?" A clerk walked over, flipped through a few books, and gave him a disdainful look, asking lazily.

"You tell me!"

"No, it's your stuff, you should say it yourself."

"Five yuan!" Seeing the fellow's disdainful and dismissive attitude, he didn't dare to ask for more.

"No," the clerk said bluntly.

"According to you, how much is it worth?"

"One yuan!"

He was so frightened that he almost jumped up, wanting to slap the clerk heavily. Books worth ten yuan are only worth one yuan! This is really a joke. He probably thinks these books were stolen from someone else's house! Even if I'm destitute, I can't auction them off at such a low price. When I bought them back then, it took a lot of effort to get them.

"So cheap? At least three yuan..."

"No!" The clerk turned around and walked away with a disapproving look.

He angrily left the bookstore, feeling extremely humiliated. A ball of angry flames was burning fiercely in his heart, as he walked with a large bundle of books in the bustling street.

Short Story

The Same Hopelessness 222

— Han Gu Nong, a Thirteen-Year-Old Elementary School Student

The autumn wind blew through the withered treetops, making rustling sounds. At this time, the rice in the fields had all been harvested, and the village was filled with the sound of threshing rice. It was the time of the autumn harvest. In a corner of this village, there was a thatched cottage, the house of tenant farmer Zhang San. At this time, there were three children, asking Zhang San. One was about thirteen or fourteen years old, and the other was about six or seven years old, probably his sons. They had returned from the fields and were making requests to their father.

"Dad! It's time to buy me new clothes. Li Rongguan, from the landlord's family in the next village, is already wearing his new clothes," said the thirteen or fourteen-year-old son, looking at his father.

"Dad! When will you buy me the little foreign doll in the foreign goods store on the street?" The six or seven-year-old child also shouted.

"Children! Don't make a fuss! Where do we have the money to buy luxury goods?" the father said heavily, sighing.

"Father, didn't we harvest a lot of rice? Sell it and we'll have a lot of money," asked the older child in disbelief.

"We still have to pay rent, and we still have to pay back the money we owe people. And this year there's a war, and our cattle were taken away by the army. We haven't paid off the money yet," the old farmer explained to the two children in detail.

"I want a foreign doll... I want new clothes too. Anyway, we had a good harvest this year, right?" the children still pleaded.

"Although the harvest was good this year, we harvested three stones per mu, but because the harvest was good, we couldn't sell it for a good price, only selling for six or seven yuan per stone. In terms of calculation, it's not as good as the flood last year. Alas! Only those who do business make money. Where do I have the money to buy you these things? Look! How many holes are there in the clothes I'm wearing?"

"Why is that Li Rongguan dressed so beautifully, but we don't have anything?"

"Because they have money and property, so they have everything."

"If they have money, why do they still want us to pay them rent?"

"Don't say too much. It's getting late, you should quickly take the cattle to graze. We'll buy you your things when the harvest is better next year!"

"A better harvest, isn't it still the same hopelessness!"

The child said…

Film Special

Anecdotes of the Film Stage

The Beginning of Cinema 223

— Shi Fo

Cinema originated in the West. The Book of Han records that Emperor Wu's concubine, Lady Li, passed away, and the Emperor was deeply saddened. A Taoist magician from Qi, Shao Weng, claimed he could summon her spirit. He set up lamps and candles at night, arranged curtains and tents, and displayed wine and meat, while having the Emperor reside in another tent. From afar, he could see a beautiful woman resembling Lady Li, returning to the tent, sitting and walking; but he could not approach and see her clearly. The Emperor became more and more reminiscent and sad, composing a poem saying, "Is it her? Is it not her? Standing and gazing, why is she so slow to come!" He ordered the musicians of the Music Bureau to sing it. Later, Emperor Wu wrote an ode mourning Lady Li, saying, "…her demeanor graceful and elegant, drifting and swaying, becoming more dignified; gracefully leaning and touching the pillars, continuously glancing with beautiful eyes." All these describe the forms seen in a trance. Today's cinema is just like that. The Records of the Capital City state that shadow plays were initially made by people in the capital using plain paper carvings, later using colored leather. The loyal were carved with righteous faces, and the treacherous with ugly faces. This is similar to the making of lantern shadows. From this perspective, could cinema have originated in our country?

Sound cinema was invented by the American Edison, making rapid progress to what it is today. We cannot but admire the Westerners' rapid progress in creating and improving any undertaking. I remember when cinema in Shanghai was not yet developed, and the films shown were very childish. Now, movie theaters stand in rows, not inferior to those in the West, and the films shown are mostly new releases. Shanghai is truly the second Paris! Even in terms of domestic films, although they cannot compare with foreign ones, the speed of progress is truly amazing. Who wouldn't call it a good phenomenon?

Since we cannot travel around the world to broaden our horizons, the only remedy is to watch movies. For a small price, we can virtually travel to famous cities around the world, beautiful wildernesses, ancient ruins of Egypt and Persia, and the wonders of deserts and polar regions. This is why I like to watch scenic films, firstly. In this toiling world, only emotions can regulate the monotonous life. Watching appropriate romance films can fill the emotional sky, level the sea of hatred, and enhance the love between couples. This is why I like to watch romance films, secondly. In this world where people's hearts are becoming depraved, demons are capturing people, shadows are everywhere, and danger lurks everywhere, watching detective films can inspire thinking and broaden new knowledge. This is why I like to watch detective films, thirdly. In remote and exotic lands, steep cliffs and vast oceans, adventurers travel around, both increasing the courage to take risks and gaining a wide range of knowledge. This is why I like to watch adventure films, fourthly. However, domestic films that can meet the above four points are not easy to find often, which is why foreign films are popular.

Colbert's Costume Image 224

—

We have introduced the new film Sign of the Cross, directed by Cecil B. DeMille, many times. The female lead he was looking for was ultimately Claudette Colbert. She can be considered a newcomer. We first saw her

in Herschel's fourth work, Playboy of Paris, playing a not-so-important female role. However, at that time, many people already recognized her talent, and today she was indeed selected by Cecil B. This figure is Claudette Colbert's expression in Roman attire.

Film Review

[Woman from Monte Carlo] 225

— Yan Nan

Monte Carlo gives us a deep impression, not because geography tells us that it is a city in Monaco, but because MacDonald and Buchanan tell us on film that it is a gambling city with excellent scenery. Now Carlton's Woman From Monte Carlo is released. Because of the suggestion of the four words Monte Carlo, many people hope to see what it is all about?

The protagonist is the European old lover, Lilj Dagover. She was hired to Hollywood, and this is her first production. She can perform a plot that is usually narrated just right. She has taken on more than half of the work in almost every play, giving the audience extreme satisfaction. The male protagonists Walter Huston and Warren William perform the beauty of red flowers and green leaves.

The plot is very simple, just showing a scene of tragedy at sea. Because of the dispute in love, it caused great misfortune, and the war between the two ships was used as the focus of the outbreak of this tragedy. It clearly pointed out that women are a source of trouble, enough to affect everything. In the courtroom scene, love, filth, friendship, hate, emotion, reason, and responsibility were used to collide face-to-face, creating a very high peak. This is the achievement of the director's skill. At the end, the beautiful scenery of Monte Carlo and the prosperous singing and dancing were used to make the tense and tragic situation change sharply, forming a kind of leisurely elegance, like a wry smile, lingering in the minds of the audience. The superficial calm reflects the past, giving us deeper memories and emotions!

There are many magnificent sets, especially in the scene where the battleship sinks.

The organization, light, and photography are all good. The dialogue is even more commendable. Almost every word will run to our ears. This is not entirely because the sound is clear, but because most of its actors are British, so they speak honest and pure language, which invisibly increases the power of the performance.

In short, from the proof of this film, the products of First National Company have made great progress.

Overseas News: Peng Kai's Return to the Screen 226

— Xing

Velma Bánky and Harry Liedtke have been separated from us for more than three years. Since marrying Rod LaRooque, although many newspapers and private letters have requested her to act, she has ultimately resolutely abandoned the screen and lived a fulfilling family life.

News came that this summer, she suddenly signed a contract with Universal Pictures and made a comeback to the camera. The film is titled Ihe Robel, directed and starring Luis Trenker from [The Battle of the Gate].

Please don't misunderstand. A female star's return to the screen after marriage is not necessarily due to divorce or other unfortunate events. Because if you use this general rule to speculate on Peng Kai's return to the screen, it would be a far cry from the truth. Her filming is entirely out of interest, and her husband also agrees with it.

When this film is about to be published, people will know.

It's not that Universal or she personally wants to keep any secrets, but because its interior and exterior scenes were not filmed in Hollywood. Therefore, very few people knew about this film in advance.

When Peng Kai left the screen, sound films were at their peak, so many people made many rumors, saying that her voice was not good, so she could not shoot sound films. Now? The·Rcbel is clearly a sound film, breaking another dumb puzzle.

Don't be happy, because she only signed a contract for one film. Maybe she will never be happy to shoot a second one. However, a flash in the pan is enough to comfort the fans who have been eager for her for one or two years!

Director's Little History

The Life of Steinhamm (Part 2) Ren Gong

Indeed, this barber college is not only closely related to Shi's later experience, but also extremely helpful. Gai Shi not only learned the methods of using combs and scissors, but also studied a lot of work in general decoration art; especially because he developed an aesthetic sentiment, he also had a unique understanding of [sitting and talking art]. For example, how should the main customer interact with him within a certain period of time, and then provide spiritual entertainment, transforming their strong character into gentle emotions. Like the above, these are the most important subjects for Shi in the school. In other words, this is the foundation of his success in the future.

Now, there are many people around him engaged in writing, proving that this artist of combs and scissors is an extraordinary director. Therefore, the male and female actors who appear in his films can often see the sitting and talking art that ordinary actors would not expect, forming his personal superior position in art. From this point of view, the subjects of that barber college did give Shi a great stiff power and undeniable.

When Shi was sixteen years old, he had a love affair with a girl in an apartment called Gretel. His debut feature-length comedy [Memories,] describes the circumstances of that era. Later, Shi finally suffered disappointment in love, so his views on films opposed the ideal of happy ending as the foundation. In other words, his outlook on life and love changed greatly because of this relationship.

Also, when Shi completed his barber's degree, he left the quaint university district and the washerwoman's mother, and decided to come to the capital Berlin. Naturally, it is very difficult for a person from the interior to find a job in a metropolis for the first time. Shi also could not avoid this example. He first carried coal, and then worked as a post office messenger, a barber at the prison, an inspector, and a road worker, etc., with as many as thirty-eight kinds of famous and infamous occupations. Finally, he wanted to engage in the most infamous [active actor], but who knew that this was an inhuman life, which can also be said to be the behavior of a blasphemer, so the result was still hopeless.

At that time, in 1905, there was no so-called photography studio in Berlin. If you wanted to take photos, you had to use natural light on the foundations of great buildings. If it rained, there was no way to do it. But soon, water lights were invented, allowing people to take photos freely indoors. The strength of the light is absolutely not affected by any side; in this way, there was the so-called film director system, and our comb and scissors artist, Mr. Steinhamm, began to appear under the mercury lamp from this time (1906). (End)

Mary Pickford Changed to Play a Middle-Aged Woman

Mary Pickford's most welcome and beloved feature is her beautiful curly hair, short skirt, and infinitely innocent childlike temperament, which has attracted countless viewers.

But now, Mary's youth is gradually fading away, which is the most heartbreaking thing for her. In her recent works, (Taming of the Shrew,) flirtatious women, we can no longer find these lovely situations in the two films. In short, she is not who she used to be now.

But! Why can the previous few films still be welcomed by the audience? This is nothing more than her faithful and sincere situation that can still get the audience's sympathy.

Now that she is a middle-aged woman, she has decided to change her lovely girl's dress and put on the simple and sincere dress of a middle-aged woman, and then try to return to the screen and continue to perform. But according to the general idea of the five people, her result may still be a failure.

[No,] absolutely not. She is now actively preparing and working hard to reunite with the audience who used to like her, so although she can no longer be called [the lover of the world,] at least she has to be called [the world's most faithful wife and mother.]

Film Essays

Attractive Eyesight 231

— Chen Dabei

Think again! Imagine when you are determined to become a star, a good friend suddenly cures your eye disease, immediately giving you a new pair of eyes, allowing you to see the light again. How would you welcome it? How should you cherish your newly acquired eyes from now on?

Friends, I hope you always remember that your eyes were given to you by a good friend. You should cherish this priceless gift more than anything else you own. Be sure to remember not to do anything that could harm your eyesight. Such as reading in poorly lit places, eating curry, mustard, and scallions, chives, peppers, garlic, using public face towels to wipe your eyes, and the transmission of venereal diseases, etc., all must be prevented as much as possible, and not taken lightly.

Today, after carefully examining your eyes in the mirror, you should first thoroughly understand this priceless new gift, second, carefully cherish it, and third, know how to use it.

You've been using your eyes since today, that's right. But from now on, since you are determined to walk the path of a star, you should first train your eyes to have the eyesight of a star.

The eyesight of a star is different from that of ordinary people, it must have an appeal. The eyesight of a star is the sharpest expression of all kinds of expressions and actions of the whole body. The eyesight of a star can communicate the soul of the star with the soul of the director, and with the soul of the screenwriter, and also communicate the souls of the two of them with the audience, instantly using the screenwriter's bitterness to draw the tears of the actors, and using the director's humor to make the actors laugh uncontrollably.
